      "Extract bin values from a polar radar data set at rain gage locations"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",
     "level": 4,
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "Read polar data set"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": true,
     "input": [
      "filename = wradlib.util.get_wradlib_data_file('misc/polar_R_tur.gz')\n",
      "data = np.loadtxt(filename)"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [],
     "prompt_number": 3
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",
     "level": 4,
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "Define site coordinates (lon/lat) and polar coordinate system"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": true,
     "input": [
      "r = np.arange(1,129)\n",
      "az = np.linspace(0,360,361)[0:-1]\n",
      "sitecoords = (9.7839, 48.5861)"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [],
     "prompt_number": 4
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",
     "level": 4,
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "Make up two rain gauge locations (say we want to work in Gaus Krueger zone 3)"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": true,
     "input": [
      "# Define the projection via epsg-code\n",
      "proj = wradlib.georef.epsg_to_osr(31467)\n",
      "# Coordinates of the rain gages in Gauss-Krueger 3 coordinates\n",
      "x, y = np.array([3557880, 3557890]), np.array([5383379, 5383375])"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [],
     "prompt_number": 5
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "#### Now extract the radar values at those bins that are closest to our rain gauges\n",
      "\n",
      "For this purppose, we use the PolarNeighbours class from wraldib's verify module. Here, we extract the 9 nearest bins..."
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "polarneighbs = wradlib.verify.PolarNeighbours(r, az, sitecoords, proj, x, y, nnear=9)\n",
      "radar_at_gages = polarneighbs.extract(data)\n",
      "print( \"Radar values at rain gauge #1: %r\" % radar_at_gages[0].tolist())\n",
      "print( \"Radar values at rain gauge #2: %r\" % radar_at_gages[1].tolist())"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "Radar values at rain gauge #1: [0.01, 0.01, 0.02, 0.02, 0.01, 0.01, 0.01, 0.02, 0.05]\n",
        "Radar values at rain gauge #2: [0.15, 0.2, 0.06, 0.06, 0.26, 0.69, 0.03, 0.05, 0.09]\n"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 6
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",

      "Retrieve the bin coordinates (all of them or those at the rain gauges)"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "binx, biny = polarneighbs.get_bincoords()\n",
      "binx_nn, biny_nn = polarneighbs.get_bincoords_at_points()"
     ],

     "metadata": {},

     "input": [
      "fig = pl.figure(figsize=(12,12))\n",
      "ax = fig.add_subplot(121)\n",
      "ax.plot(binx, biny, 'r+')\n",
      "ax.plot(binx_nn, biny_nn, 'b+', markersize=10)\n",
      "ax.plot(x, y, 'bo')\n",
      "ax.axis('tight')\n",
      "ax.set_aspect(\"equal\")\n",
      "pl.title(\"Full view\")\n",
      "ax = fig.add_subplot(122)\n",

      "ax.set_aspect(\"equal\")\n",
      "txt = pl.title(\"Zoom into rain gauge locations\")\n",

      "Create synthetic data and reconstruct KDP"

     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "# Synthetic truth\n",
      "dr = 0.5\n",
      "r = np.arange(0, 100, dr)\n",
      "kdp_true = np.sin(0.3*r)\n",
      "kdp_true[kdp_true<0] = 0.\n",
      "phidp_true = np.cumsum(kdp_true)*2*dr\n",
      "# Synthetic observation of PhiDP with a random noise and gaps\n",
      "phidp_raw = phidp_true + np.random.uniform(-2, 2, len(phidp_true))\n",
      "gaps = np.random.uniform(0, len(r), 20).astype(\"int\")\n",
      "phidp_raw[gaps] = np.nan\n",
      "\n",
      "# Reconstruct PhiDP and KDP\n",
      "phidp_re, kdp_re = wradlib.dp.process_raw_phidp_vulpiani(phidp_raw, dr=dr)\n",
      "\n",
      "# Plot results\n",
      "fig = pl.figure(figsize=(12,8))\n",
      "ax = fig.add_subplot(211)\n",
      "pl.plot(kdp_true, \"g-\", label=\"True KDP\")\n",
      "pl.plot(kdp_re, \"r-\", label=\"Reconstructed KDP\")\n",
      "pl.grid()\n",
      "lg = pl.legend()\n",
      "\n",
      "ax = fig.add_subplot(212)\n",
      "pl.plot(r, phidp_true, \"b--\", label=\"True PhiDP\")\n",
      "pl.plot(r, np.ma.masked_invalid(phidp_raw), \"b-\", label=\"Raw PhiDP\")\n",
      "pl.plot(r, phidp_re, \"g-\", label=\"Reconstructed PhiDP\")\n",
      "pl.grid()\n",
      "lg = pl.legend(loc=\"lower right\")\n",
      "txt = pl.xlabel(\"Range (km)\")"
